 yahi vajah he ki pakkaa sangeet aaj bhi elite tabake tak hi simata hua he

 usee kram main ab yah pustak ai he

 is tarah ke sibar hamale neuyark evam washington main brussels ke khilaaf bhi kiye gaye
 CNN was quoted as saying by the European Parliament's Speaker Martin Schultz, "I am very concerned and taken aback by these allegations
 " Schultz has stated, "if the allegations prove true, it will be a very serious matter, which will have a profound effect on EU-US relations
" europea sansad kii ore se main america prashasan se in aaropon ke sambandh main tatkaal purna spashtikaran chahta hum
 " germany ke nyaay mantralay ke pravaktaa anders marjaluf ke anusaar, german nyaay mantri sabeen luthesar-scanarenburger ne kaha he ki yadi aarope sach he to yah shityudh kii yaad taaja karaane vaali ghatana he
 Information published in Der Spiegel came from confidential documents obtained from former ISI employee Edward Snowden
 patrika kii report main kaha gaya he, "sitambar 2010 ke ek atyant gopneey dastavej se pataa chalata he ki enese ne kis tarah washington sthit europea sangh ke rajanyik mishan par hamalaa kiya he
 " report main kaha gaya he ki europea sangh kii imaarat main aise bags lagaae gaye hai, jo aantarik computer network main ghuskar sari jaankaree hasil kar lete hai

 der spigal kii report par washington kii ore se tatkaal koi jawaab nahin aayaa he

 Valentine's Day 2019 Make Up Tips: Valentines Day is about to knock
 sabhi par pyaar kaa khumaar chaaya hua he
 People make a lot of preparations to impress their crush or partner
 vailemtine de ke din sabase best dikhne ke liye log apni luks par bhi kaaphi dhyaan dete hai
 Women suffer the tension of the right makeup with their clothes, because even if the makeup is not right, expensive and nice dress would not make their look good
 lekin aapako pareshaan hone kii jarurat nahin hai, ham aapako vailemtine de ke liye kuch best mechap tips bataa rahe hai, jinhen follow kar ke aap is vailemtine de apni luk se kisi ko bhi impress kar sakengi
 Step 1: Before applying foundation, apply primer on face
 isse aapke chehre ke porce chhip jate hai or mechap der tak tikaa rahata he
 Step 2: There are some very small spots on everyone's face
 lekin in daag-dhabbon se aapaki khubsuurati main koi kami naa aae iske liye mechap karne se pehle chehre kii rednes ko chhipaane ke liye usapar hare rang kaa concillar lagaaein or dark sarkals par peach rang kaa concilkar lagaaein
 Step 3: Apply a foundation on the face with the help of a makeup blender or brush
 foundation apni skin color se ek shed dark hi chune
 Step 4: Now fix your foundation with face powder
 powder lagane se aapkaa mechap lambey samay tak set rahata he
 Step 5: Eyes often say things which words cannot say
 vailemtine de din apni ankhon kaa mechap karte samay khaas dhyaan rakhen
 On this day, give eyes a light smokey look with metallic colored eyeshadow
 dhyaan rakhen ki ai mechap naa bahut zyada ho or naa bahut kam
 Step 6: Makeup is incomplete without lipstick
 vailemtine de ke din red yaa pink shed kii lipstick hi chune
 Bold dark shade lipstick enhances facial glow to make you stand out in a crowd of people
 ek boij home main rahane vaale bacchon ke saath aprakritik yon sambandh banane va unka shoshan karne ke aarope main ravivaar ko ek isai padri ko giraftaar kiya gaya he
 An official of the Palluruthi police station, on the condition of anonymity, said that the pastor of the shelter home has been arrested on the basis of a complaint by the parents of the children
 unhone kaha, 'bacchon ke mata-pita kii shikaayat ke aadhaar par padri ko uthaa liya gaya or ravivaar ko uski giraftaar hui
 'according to the complaint of the parents of seven children, the pastor had been sexually abusing the children for a long time
 bacchon ke mata-pita kii shikaayat ke anusaar, jab padri ne bacchon ke kathith yon utpeedan kii koshish kii to bachche vahaan se bhaag gaye
 He said the pastor had been allegedly sexually assaulting six children since December last year
 padri girjaghar dwaara sanchalit ladakon ke aashray grih kaa nideshak tha
 In this shelter, children of poor families are provided with living facilities and education
 police ne bataaya ki yah maamla us samay saamne aayaa jab aashray grih ke chah bachche vahaan se bhaag gaye or unhone shanivaar kii raat raste main mili ek vyakti kii madad se apane mata-pita ko phone kiya
 He said charges have been framed against the pastor under relevant sections of Juvenile Justice Act and Protection of Child Sexual Offenses (POCSO)
 kendriya arun jetali ne kaha ki pakistan ke andar ghuskar jaish-e-mohammad ke aatanki shiviron par safaltaapurvak hawaii hamalaa kar bharat ne pakistan ke parmaanu dhauns kii kalai khol di he
 In a news channel program on Saturday, Jaitley said, "pakistan fought the Conventional War (traditional war) 1965, 1971 with India
 kargil yuddh main ve apane sainikon kii laashen tak lene nahin aae or haar gaye
 So the Pakistani army saw that we cannot stand in front of India's strong economy and superior military strength in the Conventional War
 " unhone kaha ki unke saamne do vikalp the- ek, aatankwaadiyon ke jariye proxi waar (chhadam yuddh) or doosraa vikalp jise newclear blf (parmaanu dhauns) kehete hai, kyonki donon deshon ke paas atomi hathiyaar hai
 This time his nuclear bluff was also exposed
 pakistan ke balakot main bhartiya vayusena dwaara hawaii hamale main jaish aatankiyon ke maare jane ke saboot maangane par jetali ne vipakshi dalon par nishaanaa saadhaa
 He said, "political parties and leaders should understand that no army in the world makes public its operational details
 ye desh kaa durbhaagya he or kuch netaaon main is prakaar kii nasamajhi he ki ve aaj saarvajanik jivan main hai
 They are becoming witnesses of Pakistan by making such statements, knowingly and unknowingly
 mujhe lagata he ki janata inkaa wo haal karegi ki pakistan ke tivi main inako tiarapy milegi or hindustan main janata kaa aakrosh bardaasht karnaa hoga
 "the widows of the martyrs of the Pulwama attack, although not the details of the action, are asking for any picture of the slain terrorists
" ve kah rahi hai ki koi tasviir hi dikhaa diya jaataa to unke dil ko thandak pahunchati
 It is not impossible to provide a picture with the help of satellite
 jetali ne kaha, "duniya main kahin bhi koi army yaa air force apane oparational ditels saarvajanik nahin karti
 The US attacked in Abbottabad (pakistan), killed Al Qaeda Chief Osama bin Laden and threw his body into the sea and shared no operational details from the world
 "bhartiya vayusena ke hawaii hamale kii safalataa par sawaal uthaanewaale congress netaa kapil sibbal par nishaanaa sadhate hue jetali ne kaha, "ye durbhagyapurna he ki aise log saarvajanik jivan main hai
 If Operation Details were made public, not only Kapil Sibal, Pakistan's army would also know how many of our Mirage flew, where it flew, how many bombs were fired and by which way the terrorist camp was targeted
 " unhone kaha ki vah pakistan kii sena hi thi na ki vahaan ki sarkaar jisane sabase pehle hawaii hamale kii jaankaree logon ko di
 Pakistan first informed the world about the strike
 
 He said that there were two main reasons behind this
 pehla, pakistan main unki fouj ne janata ke bich apni badi chhavi banaai hui he
 How could that country go in front of its citizens and say that Indian airplanes bombed Jaish's camp
 jetali ne kaha ki doosraa kaaran or bhi bada he
 If Pakistan complained to the whole world, see that Indian planes violated our loc, then the first question would arise - what was your loss? Then the international community would see the loss
 
 Which camp was going on there? How many buildings were there in the camp and hundreds of people were staying
 
 Swimming pool
 
 There was a gymnasium
 
 Those who died there would ask about them
 
 Who were those people? 
 One by one, the names of their BC commanders and old and new fidayeen were revealed
 jetali ne kaha, "pakistan ke saath tab tak koi baatcheet nahin ho sakati, jab tak vah aatanki sanghathanon ke khilaaf koi nirnaayak karrwai nahin karegaa
 That action should be seen by the whole world and Pakistan will give proof of that, then we will think what to do
 abhi baatcheet ke liye awaajen uthaane kaa koi auchity nahin he
 " mata vaishno devi ke aadhaar shivi katra ke liye sidhe jane vaali nai train katra railway stesan ke paas ingine kharaab hone ke kaaran ek surang main funs gai
 Shree Shakti Express, a fully air-conditioned superfast train from New Delhi to Katra, was running on this route for the second time, but the incident occurred five kilometers before the station
 ek din pehle hi train ko nai dilli se shuru kiya gaya tha
 Ferozepur division railway manager (DRM) NC Goel said that the train reached Katra at 7 am
 haalanki iske vahaan pahunchane kaa samay subah 5
 It was 10 o'clock
 ferozepur mandal ke antargat hi jammu kashmir kaa rail network aata he
 Railway sources said that the Sri Shakti Express from New Delhi to Katra got stuck in the tunnel five kilometers before reaching Katra at its destination, as the train engine in the tunnel was damaged
 train ek ghante tak surang main fansi rahi
 Being a new station, the engine was brought from Udhampur at Katra railway station
 haal hi main pradhanmantri narendra modi ne yahaan se train seva kaa shubharambh kiya tha
 DRM Goyal of Ferozepur division said that he was waiting for information about the reasons for the delay in the operation of the train and engine malfunction
 unhone bataaya ki train tay samay se 100 minute kii deree se gantavy sthaan tak pahunch gai
 The train was delayed by about 35 minutes and about an hour wasted due to engine failure in the tunnel located just five kilometers from Katra railway station

 to samaj nahin paae galati kiski he
 Raj's sister Riya Patel told us' My brother Raj is suffering from schizophrenia, so we kept him in a separate room
 kyonki kai baar hamen dar lagata tha ki wo zyada hinsak hokar building se chalaang naa laga de
 We have never beaten him
 ' The head of the family is Rishabh Patel, with ten children in total from the first and second wife, once upon a time there was a large plastic factory in Gujarat, later the money invested in the factory and the stock market was drowned
 khud dane-dane ko mohataaz hai, ghar main kamare kai hai, lekin naa to bijli he

 ' Raj, who weighs 25 kg at the age of 22, is hospitalized
 ek enjio kii shikaayat par use ghar se nikaala gaya, lekin police kaa kahana he ki parivaar khud badahaali main he, aise main us par sangdili kaa aarope thik nahin
